TERI is a not-for-profit research organisation working on issues related to energy, environment, climate change, and sustainable development. The Education for Youth Empowerment (EYE) Area at TERI works with school students and youth to promote Education for Sustainable Development (ESD) in India and abroad.
 
To foster a community of young innovators dedicated to creating solutions that mitigate effects of climate change, the 5th edition of the 'Youth Climate Conclave' (YCC) is being convened. The conclave features a series of pre-event activities in the age category of 10â€“18 years and 19â€“25 years, including a photography competition, a two-day knowledge enrichment session (aligned with TERI's World Sustainable Development Summit 2025), and an exclusive excursion to provide evidence-based learning to empower youth to combat climate change.
 
We invite children and youth in the age category of 10-18 years and 19-25 years to participate in a Photography Competition. Attractive awards and incentives are in store for top performers.
 
Please find attached the competition guidelines and a poster.  To register and submit entries for the competition, click on this link: https://wsds.teriin.org/2025/youth-climate-conclave-5.php. The deadline to submit the entry is 1st October 2024.
 
For any further information, please feel free to write to us at youthclimateconclaveedition5@gmail.com/ monmi.barua@teri.res.in or visit https://wsds.teriin.org/2025/youth-climate-conclave-5.php

13/10/24, 12:04â€¯pm - Rakesh Anna SNUC: Ah we are planning for a workshop explaining these


U will also have a shutter speed which plays a major role


ISO is basically set by international standardisation organisation 

Which determines the sensitivity of the sensor of the camera greater the iso more light it absorbs


WB is white balance

It determines how the colour white will look in the picture 
Its measured in kelvins

Like if u keep it warm the white will be red (like blue light filter in mobiles, it makes pic warm) and if its cold the whites will be blue


And ev is exposure its basically how dark or bright you want your photos to be
I like my picture dark so i keep it in -1 (personal taste)


There shld be shutter speed shich has a major role in all pictures

10/01/25, 5:49â€¯pm - Rakesh Anna SNUC: Guys, 
The rule of thirds-
This may seem like a bit technical and boring title but trust me this is the best way to step up your photography.

*Always use grid lines*
Dharani is the specialist in framing techniques and i started to learn em one by one.
This was the first one i tried though it may feel dumb at start, eventually you will notice a unique definition in your pictures


Try to find the main object you wanna capture like a subject (tree, pot , cup) and make it come under one of the four intersection points or in the one third frame of the whole picture.


This also works for the insta aesthetic people to have _aesthetic captions_


Since y'all are in your holiday  and a festival is coming up try to practice this technique as much as you can <This message was edited>
